 Palamu district is 127 years old, is associated with Mahabharata period History of Palamu district is 127 years old
 1 janvari 1892 ko palamu ko jila ghoshit kiya gaya tha
 Earlier, after the Revolt of 1857, it was a subdivision with headquarters at Daltonganj
 1871 main pargana japalaa or beluja ko gaya se palamu main sthanantarit kar diya gaya tha
 The early history of Palamu is full of legends and traditions
 swytt janajatiyaan shaayad ateet main kshetra kaa nivas karti thim
 Kharwar, Oraon and Chero ruled Palamu
 palamu kaa itihaas mughal kaal se adhik pramanik he
 Palamu was also known as Mughal Paloon or Paloon
 aaj ke samay main palamu kii seemaa bihar se chooti he
 The local language of Palamu is Nagpuri
 palamu main jile kaa mukhyalay medininagar he
 It has 22 blocks
 ye hai - medininagar, channpur, ramgarh, satabarwa, leslieganj, panki, talahasi, manaatu, patan, pandva, vishrampur, nava bazaar, pandu, utari, mohammadganj, haidernagara, hussainabad, chhatarpur, hariharganj, naudiha or pipara

 There is a place in the world where the sun hides at 12:43 pm and rises at a mere 40 minutes
 yah najaara norway main dekhne ko miltaa he
 Here the sun hides at midnight and birds start chirping at around half past one
 ye silsilaa ek-do din nahin, saal main kareeb dhai maheenaa yahaan suraj chhipata hi nahin
 Hence it is called 'country of Midnight Sun'
 76 dinon tak yahaan suraj ast nahin hota
 
 
 This is how the beauty of Norway is made
 iskaa shumaar duniya ke amir mulkon main hota hai
 The special thing is that the people here are very comfortable about health
 healdi khaanaa pasand karte hai
 Among all these things, Norway's greatest quality is its natural beauty
 ye desh architik sarkal ke andar aata he
 The sun does not set here for about 76 days between May and July
 beshak is anubhav ko vahaan jaakar hi mahasoos kiya ja saktaa he
 The incident takes place in the town of Heimerfest, at the northern end of Norway
 jahaan 100 saalon se suraj nahin niklaa
 
 
 There is also a city in this unique country at one end of the world where the sun has not been seen for 100 years
 isaki vajah shahar kaa chaaron tarah se pahaado se ghira hona he
 However, the engineers there have created a 'new sun' with the help of glass to solve this problem
 is artificial suraj ko pahari par is tarah se lagaaya gaya he ki vah dhoop ko shahar tak pahunchaata he or khud ek suraj ke jaise lagata he
 Its light falls directly on the town square
 yahi vajah he ki yah jagah logon ko aakarshith karti hai
 Know about the 5 countries of the world, where it does not set up for the sun and astronomical reasons, as you know that the Sun is stable in space and the Earth completes one orbit in its orbit i
e
 365 days
 saath hi wo apane aksh yani dhuree par 24 ghante main ek chakkar puraa karti he
 Because of this revolution of the Earth's sun, there are days and nights
 lekin din or raat kii avadhi hameshaa baraabar nahin hoti
 Sometimes the days are big and the nights are short, sometimes the days are short and the nights are big
 darasal ye prithvi ke aksh ke jhukaav kaa nateeja he
 Let us tell you that there is no real axis of the Earth
 jab prithvi gumti he to ek uttar or doosraa dakshin main aise do bindu banate hai, jinhen ek sidhi rekha se jod diya jaae to ko ek dhuree banati he thik vaise hi jaise cycle ke pahiyon kii dhuree hoti he
 On which they rotate, the earth rotates at an angle of 66 degrees from its plane, due to which the axis of the earth is not perpendicular to 23 degrees
 aksh ke jhukaav ke kaaran hi din va raat chote-bade hote hai

 The government will introduce this bill called 'the Muslim Women Protection of Rights in Marriage Act'
 ye kanoon sirf teen talaak (INSTANT TALAQ, yani talaak-e-biddat) par hi lagu hoga
 After this law, if any Muslim husband gives three divorces to the wife, then it will be illegal
 bataa den ki isi saal 22 agast ko supreme court ne teen talaak ko gaiyr kanoonee qaraar diya tha

 1 disambar ko draft taiyaar kar rivyuu ke liye bheja gaya tha, or 10 disambar tak suzav maanga tha

 bill ko jharkhand, assam, madhyapradesh, maharashtra, manipur or uttar pradesh jaise rajyon kaa samarthan mila he
 Explain that three divorces granted in any form under the bill, whether oral or written or in a message, would be illegal
 jo bhi teen talaak degaa, usko teen saal kii sajaa or jurmaana ho saktaa he

 The problem of joint pain is seen more in the elderly as soon as winter comes
 jaise-jaise sardi badhati he dard main bhi vruddhi hoti he
 Doctors believe that due to the decrease in temperature, the veins of the joints shrink and the blood temperature in that part decreases, due to which the joints become stiff and painful
 doctoron ke anusaar, kuch saavdhaaniyaan barat kar is pareshaani se bachaa ja saktaa he
 Principal of Kanpur Medical College, Orthopedic Dr
 anand swaroop ne ieenes se kaha, "thand ke mausam main hamaare dil ke aasapaas rakt kii garmaahat banaae rakhana aavashyak hota he
 Due to this, the blood supply to other parts of the body decreases
 jab twachaa thandi hoti he to dard kaa asar adhik mahasoos hota he
 This pain is called arthritis in scientific language
 "unhone kaha, "arthritis aamtaur par 40 saal se adhik umr ke logon or inamen bhi visheshkar mahilaon ko sabase zyada prabhavit karata he
 Since the knees carry the weight of the entire body, they suffer the most due to the problem of arthritis
 "doctor ne aage kaha, "rumetoid arthritis main jodon ke saath kuch duusare ang yaa puraa sharir bhi prabhavit hota he
 Pain, swelling, curvature, muscle weakness, fever, etc
 are symptoms
 "anand swaroop ne kaha ki "umr ke saath haddiyon se calcium or anya khanij padaartho kaa ksharan hone lagata he
 Bones do not come in contact in any joint
 jodon ke bich main ek cartillage kaa kushan hota he
 As we get older, the lubricant that keeps the cushion flexible and smooth begins to decrease
 ligaments kii lambaai or lacheelaapan bhi kam ho jaataa he, jisaki vajah se jod akad jate hai
 Regular exercise and nutritious diet can help you maintain joint agility
 "subah kii gunguni dhoop ko vitamin di kaa ek acha strot mana jaataa he
 This has been proved in many studies
 thand ke dinon main yadi vitamin di kii bharpoor khuraaq lee jaae to qamar dard or jodon ke dard main kaaphi aaraam miltaa he
 Sunlight also increases our body's resistance
 dhoop main baithne se raktashodh badhata he or jodon ke dard or sujan se mukti milti he
 Many important asanas or yoga, such as giddhasana and pranayama help in joint pain
 lagaataar kai ghanton tak ek hi kursi or computer ke aage baithe-baithe aapke jod akad jate hai, isliye jaruri he ki aap apane jodon ke liye thodaa vakt nikaalen
 Dr
 swaroop ke anusaar, khan-paan, marnig walk, kuch asana va kasarat jodon ko majboot rakhane main madad kar sakate hai
 Exercise and yoga under the supervision of a patient specialist
 offis main har aadhe ghante yaa ek ghante main seat chhodkar saat minute ke liye ghume-phiren
 Stretch the body
 mahilaayein oonchi hill kii sandels pahanane se bachein
 This also affects the heel, knee and calf along with the waist

 purv captain kapil dev ne kaha ki 'dhoni kii hi tarah viraat kohli bhi acchhee captaini kar rahe hai
 Both give their hundred percent
 dhoni ne kaaphi saalon tak team india kii test team kii kaman ko sambhala he
 But now everyone's eyes are on Kohli after he retired from Test cricket
 kaise wo team india ko aage badhaate hai
 Kapil said that 'there is a difference of day and night in the thinking of Dhoni and Kohli, and both left no stone unturned to win the team and make the number one team
 lekin dhoni or kohli main ek cheez samaan he ki wo har test match ko jeet ke liye apana sau fisadi dete hai
 'ashwin's best performance has been the best performance of Indian spinner r Ashwin in the recently played Test matches
 unhone gend or balle se jabardast pradarshan kiya he

 maujuuda daur main wo team india ke sabase zyada wicket lene vaale gendbaaj bhi hai

 jo team india ke salaami ballebaaj shikhar dhawan ke baraabar hai

 tabhi se unka pradarshan shandaar rahaa he
 i never thought that would go so far
 harbhajan singh bhartiya team main shandaar gendbaaji kar rahe the

 lekin tabhi achaanak aswin ne wicket lene ke saath- saath ran banaan bhi shuru kiye
 i think Ashwin is one of the most important players of Team India 'turning to be held at Green Park

 pehla match bhartiya team ke liye behad mahatvapurn hone vaala he

 aise main momentem hasil karne ke liye pehla test match kaaphi mahatvapurn hoga

 'kapil ne diya team india ko jeet mantrabhartiya test team ke purv captain kapil dev ne team india ko jeet kaa mantra diya he unhone kaha he ki 'team india ke khilaadiyon ko cricket ke brand kaa majaa lenaa chahie or shandaar cricket khel jeet hasil kerani chahie
 Because the result of this match will be out in three, four, or five days and winning the 500th historic Test match will be a very memorable and unique feeling for the players
 ' While increasing crime in Uttar Pradesh has become a big challenge for the state government, on one side there is a village where 'ramraj' is established in Kaliyuga
 is gaanv main aazaadee ke chah dashak bitne ke baad bhi koi aparaadh nahin hua he
 We are talking about the village of Behera in Naxal-affected Sonbhadra district of Uttar Pradesh
 aazaadee ke baad se aaj tak yahaan marpet, faujadaari, chori, lut, apharan yaa hatya jaisi koi aapraadhik ghatana nahin hui he
 It is not that only people of Bahra village with a population of 700 are claiming to be crime-free
 police ke record bhi unke daavon par muhar lagaate hai
 In the records of Rampur Bakonia police station, this village is absolutely impeccable since the time of independence
 jile ke varisht police adheekshak subhash chandra dube kaa kahana he ki naksaliyon se ghire hone ke baavjood is gaanv main ek bhi praathmiki darj na hona kaaphi khushi kii baat he
 According to Dubey, despite being backward, Bahera village is indeed an ideal village
 is gaanv ke logon ne duniya ke saamne ek misaal kaayam kii he
 Behera village may have been crime-free for years, but it is not that people like other villages do not have mutual estrangement
 agar kabhi kisi ke bich manmutav ho bhi gaya to gaanv ke bade-bujurg or panchayat, gaanv kii sarhad ke andar hi maamla sulajhza dete hai yani thane jaakar report likhavane kii naubat nahin aati
 Lalmani, a villager, said, "like other villages, there is rift among people in our village too, but we do not go to the police station and raise the issue with the elders of the village
 bade-bujurg jo faisla karte hai, donon paksh khushi-khushi use sweekaar kar lete hai
 "comments ek anya gramin siyaaraam ne kaha, "bade-bujurgon kaa sammaan or unke prati bharosa jataae jane ke kaaran aas-paas ke ilaake main hamaare gaanv ko vishisht pahchaan mili he
 " sonbhadra shahar se kareeb 50 kilometre dur bahera gaanv kii aabaadi kaa 30 pratishat hissaa brahman or kshatriya birdari kaa he
 Dalits and other castes constitute 70 percent of the population
 gaanv ke zyaadaatar log kheti karte hai or kai gharon ke log sarkari va nijee companiyon kii naukariyon main hai

 Senior Superintendent of Police of the district, Subhash Chandra Dubey, says that despite being surrounded by Naxalites, not having a single FIR lodged in this village is a matter of great pleasure
 dube ke mutabik, pichhadaa hone hone ke baavjood bahera gaanv vastav main ek adarsh gaanv he
 The people of this village have set an example in front of the world
 bahera gaanv bhale hi varsho se aparaadh-mukt rahaa ho, lekin aisa nahin he ki duusare gaanvon kii tarah yahaan ke logon main aapasi manmutav nahin hota he
 Even if there is an estrangement between someone, the elders and the panchayat of the village resolve the matter within the border of the village, that is, there is no need to go to the police station and write a report
 ek gramin laalamani ne kaha, "duusare gaanv kii tarah hamaare gaanv main bhi logon ke bich manmutav hota he, lekin ham maamle ko lekar thane par na jaakar gaanv ke bade-burjugon ke paas mudda rakhte hai
 The elders who decide, both sides happily accept it
 "tippaniyan Another villager Siyaram said, "our village has got a distinct identity in the surrounding area due to the respect and trust of the elders
 " The Brahmin and Kshatriya fraternity comprises 30 per cent of the population of Bahera village, about 50 km from Sonbhadra city
 70 pratishat aabaadi dalit evam anya jatiyon kii he
